Too much of what is called love is fish love.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① too much of ... 太多...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">You're asking <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></strong></em> him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你对他要求<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">过分</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">You cannot demand <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></em></strong> him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你不能要求他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太多</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>This is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></em></strong> a burden to just put on young people's shoulders.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">这对年轻人来说，负担<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太多</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>But we ask <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></em></strong> our hospitals.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">但我们对医院的要求<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太多</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">There's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></em></strong> you. There‘s not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">too much of</span></em></strong> me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太多</strong>了，我不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">多</strong>啊…</p></section><section data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfgSMBYHoS4rJibRiauPCkyxnc4lrFM6EiceynZopCJMibzianxtzutLibDXAnbbctXvoqlHjzMHIZLJCwA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="553" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《酒吧五杰》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿拓展：too much of a good thing</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">事情好得过了头；过犹不及</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Too much of </span></em></strong>a good thing is a bad thing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">一件事<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太好</strong>的话就是坏事了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② what is called love 看作一个整体：被称之为爱的.../所谓爱情</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">what is called ... 所谓...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">What is called</span></em></strong> resignation is confirmed desperation.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">所谓</strong>听天由命, 正是肯定的绝望。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">③ fish love 于鱼之爱/爱鱼之爱→自爱</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">“年轻人，为什么你要吃掉那条鱼？”</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">“因为我爱鱼”年轻人回答道。</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">“为什么你爱鱼，还要把它从水中抓出来，杀掉然后煮熟呢？不要对我说你爱鱼，你只是爱你自己，你只是觉得那条鱼吃起来很美味，所以你才抓它然后杀掉煮熟。”</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. an external love 爱的外在表现</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">external adj. 外部的；外面的；外在的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">反义词：internal 里面的；内部的；内心的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">Many <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">external</span></em></strong> influences can affect your state of mind.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">许多<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外在</strong>因素都可能影响人的心情。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">No <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">external</span></em></strong> signs, but time in the water.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">没有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外</strong>伤，但在水里泡久了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6184448" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfgSMBYHoS4rJibRiauPCkyxnx4dpjVD5iaiahoYZiajMSWavVvrgSX486ObBQg0mPcbqacjEuZWuokd4g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="553" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><p border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">...to suggest impact with an <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">external</span></em></strong> object like a missile.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">这说明撞击并非来自于导弹这样的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外部</strong>对象。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3.  what I'm gonna get  →我要得到什么</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">    what I’m gonna give →我要给出什么</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">I'll tell you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">what I'm gonna</span></em></strong> give you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">我会告诉你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我要给</strong>你的东西。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">Christmas is just around the corner. I wonder <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">what I'm gonna get</span></em></strong> from my parents.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">圣诞节就要到了。我不知道父母<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">会给我什么</strong>礼物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. enable XX to...使得XX成为可能</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">en+able  </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">This will <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">enable</span></em></strong> the audience <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to</span></em></strong> sit in comfort while watching the shows</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">这样<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">能够让</strong>观众舒舒服服地坐着看表演。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. pay off （spectacularly）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pay off</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">①付清</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">It would take him the rest of his life to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pay off</span></em></strong> that loan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">他得用余生来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">还清</strong>那笔贷款。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">②得到回报/使成功</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">Sandra was determined to become a doctor and her persistence<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> paid off</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">桑德拉决心成为医生，她的坚持<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">取得了成功</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. in the long run 从长远来看 =in the long term</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">In the long run</span></em></strong>, it's not good for the country. </p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从长远来看</strong>，对国家没有什么好处。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">In the long run</span></em></strong>, it was for the best.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">长远来说</strong>，这是最好的。</p></section><grammarly-btn style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1712.25px);-webkit-transform: style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. little 英音：舌边爆破；美音：flap t+舌侧音</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">flap t/d（弹舌音）发音：</p><section></section><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">舌侧音口型图：</p><section></section><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. a matt<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">er o</span></strong>f/ be<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">f<span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ore I</span></strong>'m   <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> r+元音连读</strong></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：it's only a matter of time</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">a matter of XX   XX的问题</span></strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">History is always <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">a matter of</span></strong></em> interpretation. </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">历史总是一种阐释角度<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的问题</strong>。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: border-box;"> days she was back at work. </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">仅仅</span></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">几天后，她又回去上班了。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：as a matter of fact   其实  </span></strong></span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's not that difficult. </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">As a matter of fact</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">, it's quite easy. </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这并不那么困难，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">实际上</strong>，容易得很。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. be discovered 和 be found 语义和语感上有区别</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> ·discover : 指发现本来存在，但</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">未被认识的事物、真理或情况</span><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> ·find : 可指偶然发现，也可指经过寻找后得到或重新获得已失去的东西。强调找到的结果。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">In the 19th century, gold </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">was discovered</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> in California.</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">19世纪时，在加利福尼亚<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发现</strong>了金子。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">The police also </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">found</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> a pistol.</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">警方还<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发现</strong>了一把手枪。</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">crossroads</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6148148" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKe8YUq7TFubOSjxc1hHiatruDIWR6E3GLRsd22eT7jibBxMpsn7FUILhDM75a3TqGLStSao2Qt2W6Jg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图源《灵书妙探》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">②（人生作出重大决定的）关键时期，转折点</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a career <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">crossroads</span></em></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">事业的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">转折点</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“转折点”还可以说：a turning point/milestone</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He felt that moving out from his parents' home was a real <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">milestone</span></em></strong> in his life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他感到搬出父母家是他一生中一个真正的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">转折点</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meeting her was the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">turning point</span></em></strong> in my life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">遇到她是我人生的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">转折点</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：come to/reach the crossroads</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He has <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">reached </span></em></strong><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">a career </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">crossroads</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的事业<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发展到了一个十字路口</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>When we <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">come to the crossroads</span></em></strong> of life, we stop, look, and listen before we go.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">走到</strong>人生的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">十字路口</strong>，我们会停下来、看一看、听一听，然后再走。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>You have <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">come to the crossroads</span></em></strong> of your destiny. It is time for you to choose.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">走到了</strong>命运的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">十字路口</strong>。是时候做出选择了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKe8YUq7TFubOSjxc1hHiatruxaQw0vrQVuIkXea85LkJBkwCX283Qx0icSbk0PVGMQ7dqr89yHTk8Yw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="960" style="vertical-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I will meet him at each <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">crossroads</span></em></strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在命运的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">交叉点</strong>，我们会相遇。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6101852" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKe8YUq7TFubOSjxc1hHiatruedfFicbK6ck4HpXc7C9xMLSCHVZxojrruG6LsuiaHtTEH2nGsp8RrmxA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图源《地狱男爵2》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：without exception 无一例外；一律</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Each plant, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">without exception</span></em></strong>, contains some kind of salt.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每一种植物都含有某种盐分，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无一例外</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All students <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">without exception</span></em></strong> must take the English examination.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有学生都必须参加英语考试，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无一例外</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. damn adv. 非常，很（用于强调）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">用法：damn+adj.<br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Everything was so <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">damn</span></em></strong> expensive.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">什么东西都贵得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">要命</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The band sounded pretty <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">damn</span></em></strong> good.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这乐队听上去真是好极了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, and… you looked really <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">damn</span></em></strong> sexy in them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对，而且你穿着真的性感<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">极了</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;">情景解读</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">皮尔卡丹在一段时间的沮丧之后设计出了自己新一季的作品，他将作品展示给艾米丽看。艾米丽赞不绝口。但此时皮尔已经取消了自己之前订过的时装周的场地。大家都在为没有场地而发愁。此时艾米丽心生一计。说道，她想到了一个合适的场地，能让皮尔成为时装周的焦点。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 300px;height: 60px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频中找到跟toast有关的表达了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of XX XX的焦点；XX的红人；在XX方面广受赞誉的人；在XX方面有口碑的人</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;width: 80%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.92827" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfd7sAP6s0AfF2PFER4Fvyn8m81o7LdYheiaTaY9KicicibRqbbMcwbT2O1kwliazia05bSMTw34w2KSTyA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>:</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The performance made her <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of the festival</strong>. </p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的演出使她在会演中<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">备受推崇</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of Buckingham Palace</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">白金汉宫的红人</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">toast除了跟“吐司”有关系，还能表达什么呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be toast</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">英释：</strong> to be likely to die or be destroyed 会死；要完蛋</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：One mistake and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're toast</strong>. 要是出一次错，<strong>你就</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I'll be toast</strong> once my mom find out that I am seeing a guy 15 years older than me. 我妈要是发现我在跟一个大我15岁的人交往<strong>我就</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完蛋了</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 300px;height: 60px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/Oa2IBgMSH1XTekmOVIItt6jsU2B7Vl5PQ5n9Rd4cqNB4ykliboPDM0jkrH4btOoniaQ5LoibGicV75cMe6axlRKYfA/640?wx_fmt=png");background-size: contain;background-attachment: style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链拓展</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color:#2e4f1a;box-sizing: border-box;">能表达“红人”；“焦点”的词链还有哪些？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color:#2e4f1a;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" auto;align-self: flex-start;flex: 10 10 0%;height: auto;margin: -10px -25px -10px 0px;z-index: 1;border-top-style: solid;border-top-width: 0px;border-top-left-radius: 0px;border-top-color: rgb(62, 62, border-box;">01</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(226, 246, 213);flex: 50 50 style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(78, 177, 17);letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1.5;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">XX's pet</strong></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">XX的红人；宝贝</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达通常用在贬义的语境中。用在某人受到了特殊照顾，以至于对他人不公的情况下。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Miss Kadlec always asks Crystal. She’s <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">such a teacher’s pet</strong>.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">老师你总是提问Crystal, 她是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">老师的红人</strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: 159) 72%);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: style="box-sizing: border-box;">情景解读</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">皮尔卡丹在一段时间的沮丧之后设计出了自己新一季的作品，他将作品展示给艾米丽看。艾米丽赞不绝口。但此时皮尔已经取消了自己之前订过的时装周的场地。大家都在为没有场地而发愁。此时艾米丽心生一计。说道，她想到了一个合适的场地，能让皮尔成为时装周的焦点。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 300px;height: 60px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频中找到跟toast有关的表达了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of XX XX的焦点；XX的红人；在XX方面广受赞誉的人；在XX方面有口碑的人</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;width: 80%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.92827" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfd7sAP6s0AfF2PFER4Fvyn8m81o7LdYheiaTaY9KicicibRqbbMcwbT2O1kwliazia05bSMTw34w2KSTyA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>:</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The performance made her <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of the festival</strong>. </p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的演出使她在会演中<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">备受推崇</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the toast of Buckingham Palace</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">白金汉宫的红人</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">toast除了跟“吐司”有关系，还能表达什么呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be toast</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">英释：</strong> to be likely to die or be destroyed 会死；要完蛋</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：One mistake and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're toast</strong>. 要是出一次错，<strong>你就</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I'll be toast</strong> once my mom find out that I am seeing a guy 15 years older than me. 我妈要是发现我在跟一个大我15岁的人交往<strong>我就</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完蛋了</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 300px;height: 60px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链拓展</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color:#2e4f1a;box-sizing: border-box;">能表达“红人”；“焦点”的词链还有哪些？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color:#2e4f1a;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" rgb(46, 79, 26);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达通常用在贬义的语境中。用在某人受到了特殊照顾，以至于对他人不公的情况下。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. Reflex </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [ˈriːfleks]  美 [ˈriːfleks]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. （对刺激的）本能反应；反射（作用）；反映物；反映形式；反射光</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 本能反应的；（角）大于180度的；（光）被反射的；反折的；反省的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflex arc [解剖] 反射弧</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">conditioned reflex 条件反射</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexive 反身的；[物] 反射的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexed [植] 反折的；下弯的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexly 反射地；反省地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexive 反身代词；反身动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexivity [数] 自反性；反射度</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexion 反射；反射作用（等于reflection）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflexed 把…折转，把…折回（reflex的过去式和过去分词）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. breathe a sigh of relief 如释重负，松了口气 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sigh 英 [saɪ]  美 [saɪ]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 叹气；叹着气说；（风）呼啸，悲鸣</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 叹息，叹气；（尤指风发出的）叹息般的声音</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Relif 英 [rɪˈliːf]  美 [rɪˈliːf] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 救济；减轻，解除；安慰；浮雕</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Still, most of us volunteers breathe a sigh of relief when the season comes to a close. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">尽管如此，这个季节即将结束时，我们大多数志愿者还是松了一口气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. recovered from 恢复；恢复知觉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">recover from illness 康复 ; 生病后恢复 ; 恢复健康 ; 病后复原</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">recover from an illness 病好了 ; 回复复兴 ; 病后康复 ; 从病中复原</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It'll take her time to recover from the illness. 她康复需要时间。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. Frustration </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [frʌˈstreɪʃn]  美 [frʌˈstreɪʃn] n. 挫折</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">词根：frustrate</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. frustrate 挫败的；无益的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">frustrated 失意的，挫败的；泄气的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. frustrated 挫败；阻挠（frustrate的过去式和过去分词形式）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. frustrate 失败；受挫</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. frustrate 挫败；阻挠；使感到灰心</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He cried with anger and frustration. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他愤怒而失望地哭了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She telephoned her best friend to vent her frustration. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她打电话给自己最好的朋友来发泄她的沮丧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. Resignation </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [ˌrezɪɡˈneɪʃn]  美 [ˌrezɪɡˈneɪʃn] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 辞职；放弃；辞职书；顺从</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Resignation Letter 辞职信 ; 辞职信函 ; 申请辞职</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">词根：resign</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. resigned 顺从的；已辞职的；己放弃的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. resignedly 听从地；服从地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. resign 辞去职务</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. resigned 辞职；顺从（resign的过去分词）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. resign 辞职</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. resign 辞职；放弃；委托；使听从</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her resignation caused quite a stir. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的辞职引起很大震动。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. move beyond feeling frustrated and start feeling resigned</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Move Beyond 超越</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It may be time to move beyond pessimism. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在或许是时候告别消极和悲观了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Some would like to move beyond mere discussion. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有些人希望讨论之余有些实际行动。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. Voluntarily </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 [ˈvɒləntrəli]  美 [ˌvɑːlənˈterəli] </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. 自动地；以自由意志</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：adv. 自动地；以自由意志automatically</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I would never leave here voluntarily. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我永远不会自愿地离开这里。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The fund is voluntarily administered. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个基金是无偿管理的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: We also ha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</em> word <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">reflex</strong>. This<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> is a</em> physica<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">l a</span></span>ctio<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n or r</span></span>eaction tha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> you</span> can'<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> control. For example… Catherine?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们还提到了本能反应这个词。它指你不能控制的身体行为或反应。举个例子，凯瑟琳？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Yes?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">恩？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: There, you close<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d your</span></span> eyes. Another reflex.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你闭眼睛了。这也是本能反应。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></strong></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">An</em><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> we ha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">breathe <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</em> sigh of relief</strong>. Which means <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> feel bette<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">fter</em> something bad doesn<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span> happen. I breath<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed a</span></span> sigh <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of</em> relief when my friend <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">recovered <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">from</em></strong> her illness.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们提到了如释重负。是指坏事未发生，我们的心情也就变好了。我的朋友康复后，我如释重负。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Bu<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> we <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sigh for</strong> other reasons too. Two useful sighing words were: <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">frustration</strong> and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">resignation</strong>.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们也会因其他事情而叹气。两个和叹气有关的词是：沮丧和无奈。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></strong></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Frustration<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> is</em> the sta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">te of<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> </em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em>being frustrated. We <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">can</em> say something <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">is</em> frustrating. It's frustrating when <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</em> boss doesn't listen <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> me.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">沮丧是指垂头丧气的状态。我们可以说某事令人很沮丧。老板不听我的意见时，我就会很沮丧。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: But let's say you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">move beyond feeling frustrated and star<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> feeling resigned</strong>.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你不沮丧了却又无奈了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></strong></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Yeah, and tha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> woul<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">be</em> whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span> finally accep<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the boss will never listen <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> me. And that's when I'll resign!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的，最终我接受了老板从来不听我建议的事实，我很无奈。这也意味着我该辞职了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: To resign also means to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">voluntarily</strong> leave a job! Please, Catherine, tell me that's just another vocabulary example?!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">辞职是指自愿放弃工作。凯瑟琳，告诉我你是为了举例子才这样说的？！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Of course it is, Dan. I love my job! I only ever sigh about what, 12 times an hour?!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">当然了，丹！我热爱我的工作！我每小时只叹</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">12</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">次气。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But though Digory could no longer hear the Lion, he could see it. It was so big and so bright that he could not take his eyes off it. The other animals did not appear to be afraid of it. Indeed, at that very moment, Digory heard the sound of hoofs from behind; a second later the old cab-horse trotted past him and joined the other beasts. (The air had apparently suited him as well as it had suited Uncle Andrew. He no longer looked like the poor, old slave he had been in London; he was picking up his feet and holding his head erect.) And now, for the first time, the Lion was quite silent.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然迪格雷听不见狮子唱歌了，但仍然能看见它。它那么高大，那么明亮，将他牢牢地吸引住了。其他动物似乎也不怕它。就在这时，他听见阵马蹄声，那匹拉车的老马小跑右从他身边过去，和其他动物站到一起了（空气适合安德鲁舅舅也适合它，它看上去不再像伦敦街头可怜的老奴隶，它正扬起腿，高昂着头。）这时，狮子第一次安静下来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:我想结账离店。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接待员:您结账了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:还没有，我想现在结账。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接待员:您可以在四楼的财务部结账。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:好了，我已经结完帐了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接待员:您需要帮忙提行李吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:要是能借用一下你们的行李车，我想我自己就行。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接待员:当然可以。请稍等，我去给您拿行李车。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: I'd like to check out.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Have you settled bill?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: No. I'd like to do that now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: You can settle your bill at the Finance Department on the fourth floor.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: Okay. I've paid my bill.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Would you like some help with your luggage?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: I think I can do it myself if I can borrow your trolley.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Certainly. Just a moment, please. I'll get it for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He tried to bring that debate to a halt.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他试图使这场辩论________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">停止</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“不用则废”这个词用在稀有语种上更具有说服力。非口语性语言将濒临消失。如果幸运，稀有语言像灭绝的蝴蝶标本储藏在博物馆展厅一样保留在专家词典中。如果不幸，它将永远消失在不成文的历史记忆中。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The phrase “use it or lose it” applies to few things more forcefully than to obscure languages. A tongue that is not spoken will shrivel into extinction. If it is lucky, it may be preserved in a specialist lexicographer’s dictionary in the way that a dried specimen of a vanished butterfly lingers in a museum cabinet. If it is unlucky, it will disappear forever into the memory hole that is unwritten history.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">10.08 每日一句：That's ridiculous.</strong></p><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", !important;'><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">太荒谬了！</strong></p><p><br/></p><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section rgba(255, 222, 3, 0.55);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(175, 223, 144, 0.34);padding: 10px 10px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">May I? 可以坐吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So you're gonna... They... They meet.有两个人…他们相遇了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They almost fall in love, but the timing isn't right.差点就坠入爱河可惜时机不对。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They... They have to part.他们不得不分开。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And then... years later, they... They meet again.后来……多年后，他们重逢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They get another chance.又有另一次机会。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, but they don't know if too much time has passed.但他们不知道是不是时间已耗尽。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why do you like that? 你怎么喜欢这种故事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't know.我不知道。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't get me wrong. It's beautiful in a kind of...别误会我的意思，故事是很美。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No, it's terrible. -It's terrible.-才怪，烂透了-是很烂。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's terrible. -It's terrible.-烂透了。-烂透了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's...真是…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, it's... That's terrible.对，烂透了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a personal question... but have you ever been through anything like that? 有个私人问题……你有没有遇过这种事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Me? No. No, no. -No.-我？没有。-没有。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When I was...在我…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When I was 16...在我16岁那一年。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was completely in love with this guy.我无可救药地爱上一个人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He played guitar...他会弹吉他。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...and I ran away from home...我逃家。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...and went to San Francisco so I could go live with him.跑去旧金山和他同居。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, he convinced me I had a beautiful voice...他让我相信我的嗓音很美。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...and I dreamed of becoming a singer.而我…梦想要当歌手。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I love San Francisco.我喜欢旧金山。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, he was... He was my first love.对，他是我的初恋。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Probably the only one.可能也是唯一吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He must have been a great guy. -I don't... I don't know, l...-他一定是个好男人。-我不知道。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He may have been. It didn't last long enough for me to find out.或许是吧，交往不够久，我不得而知。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah. Truth is, l... I can't even remember what he looked like. 事实上，我根本不记得他的长相。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Really? -Yeah.-真的吗？-对啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then that's too bad.太可惜了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My dad... My dad showed up, actually.因为我爸…我爸突然出现。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You were in trouble. -He came in.-你麻烦就大了。-他跑来找我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2___________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah.没错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And he was sick, and he...后来他生病了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He had these... These dreams of me becoming a doctor, you know? 他希望我能成为医生。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, and eventually, they became my dreams too.你知道的，最后…他的梦想成了我的愿望。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was right.他是对的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, l...
